``_`` According_VBG to_TO Evans_NNPS the_DT name_NN '_POS Surra_NNP '_POS is_VBZ used_VBN by_IN the_DT natives_NNS to_TO denote_VB anything_NN rotten_JJ ,_, and_CC is_VBZ applied_VBN by_IN them_PRP to_TO a_DT dry-rot_NN ,_, such_JJ as_IN a_DT withered_JJ leaf_NN ,_, and_CC to_TO a_DT moist_NN rot_NN ,_, such_JJ as_IN a_DT putrid_JJ carcass_NN ._.
